Things that I did that helped me to get calls for the jobs that I applied for:1) Prepared a resume focusing more on the business value that my work brought in rather than simply explaining the recondite technical terms and approaches. 2) Added keywords to each job section, highlighted important terms, used a readable font and font size, removed clutter and organized content in my resume to make it easy on the eyes to catch important details.3) Only applied for jobs that matched my profile by at least 60 to 70 percent. Applying to jobs that are not well-inclined with my profile is only going to make me lose precious time that I could have used to apply for jobs that were more suitable for my profile.4) Updated my LinkedIn. Added OpenToWork. Updated my about section with an interesting personal story, added relevant experiences, courses, skills. Received recommendations, reached out to recruiters. 5) Be an early applicant. Use LinkedIn's filter to find jobs that were posted less than 24 hrs ago. 6) Look for the name of the recruiter in the job description. Send them a connection request and directly reach out to them with the resume. 7) Add skills relevant to the job on the keyword section of the job application on workday. This is very helpful in manipulating the automated resume filtering tool.8) Be more mindful when filling the job applications to suit individual demands of the role rather than blindly following a generic approach. Hope this helps people who are finding it difficult to get calls. Please remember to try different strategies when things seem to not work rather than wasting your precious mental energy on self-doubt and self-blame. It can be difficult to go through this but you are bigger than these circumstances that will eventually pass. Cheers!What more would you add to the above list? A great representation for the ‘Careers Ladder’ and the trials and tribulations of job search and career progression.The trajectory of your career isn't always as simple and direct as climbing a set of steps. These steps are laden with hot coals, broken glasses and discarded Lego in order to trip you up and make you feel you should turn back or stay where you are. And sometimes you do have to take a step back to leap forwards or even just to readjust yourself.Progression can be simplistic and other times it can be challenging. But the view from the top sure is sweet if that’s where you desire your career to go. (Appreciate not everyone wants to make it to the top, but you all want to feel satisfied with whatever step you are on in your career.)This video is also a physical representation of my weight 😅#mondaymotivation #careerdevelopment #job #careers #careerladder #career #jobsearch #careerprogression

There's no point here to feel proud rather it's a matter of Shukr (Sheer Gratitude ). Why? Just because none of us have been given any authority to be born in a religion of his choice. That's the sole discretion of One & Only Almighty Allah who decides these issues. We don't have any contribution towards such things. So from now onwards replace the word fakhar(pride) with "shukr".e.g.Thanks to Allah I am muslimThanks to Allah I am PakistaniThanks to Allah to have a wonderful & professional armyThanks to Allah for being the member of highly professional & skilled family group..Thanks to Allah for working in a prestige organizationAnd so and so forth list continues..For further clarifications & understanding, pl check following links;Iman Ki Vocabularyhttps://lnkd.in/d8tcGYtphttps://lnkd.in/dTZxWWU6https://lnkd.in/dXNAvzP4Sincerely yoursAbu Alya Salman

Web Evolution from 1.0 to 3.0In Web 1.0, also referred to as Syntactic web or read-only web, a user's involvement was confined to reading the information given by content creators. Users could not transmit information back to the #content creators. Static web pages and personal #websites are examples of Web 1.0.Web 2.0, also known as the Social Web or read-write web, facilitated interaction between web users and sites that also enabled users to engage with one another. Every user may now be a content creator, and content is distributed and shared between websites. Facebook, Youtube, Flickr, Twitter, and other well-known Web 2.0 apps are only a few examples. Web technologies such as #HTML5, #CSS3, and #Javascript frameworks such as #ReactJs, #AngularJs, #VueJs, and others enable organizations to develop new concepts that allow users to contribute more to the Social Web. Web 3.0, also known as Semantic Web or read-write-execute, is often being referred to as the future of web. #ArtificialIntelligence and #MachineLearning enable computers to analyze #data in a similar way that humans do, which aids in the intelligent generation and distribution of useful content according to a user's specific needs.___What if computers could decipher the meaning behind data?What if they can figure out "what we're interested in?"Then they can assist us in finding what we're looking for. It can recognize people, places, events, businesses, products, and movies, among other things, and it can comprehend relationships between things. Apple's Siri, Google's Cloud API, and Wolfram Alpha are all instances of Web 3.0.Web 2.5 is a notion that addresses the practical and actual progression that we are presently seeing between Web 2.0 and 3.0. Some players, like Amazon, Google, Salesforce, etc., offer a service model in cloud computing that allows developers to create online apps for their users to connect them on any device, at any time, and from anywhere.The emphasis of Web 2.5 is mostly on mobile computing and the advancement of mobile technology. Mobile computing plays a significant role in engaging a bigger audience via native and #mobile web applications. As a result, we are seeing an increasing number of apps enter the mobile market to build their presence by targeting mobile consumers. Progressive Web Apps (#PWA), Accelerated Mobile Pages (#AMP), and other technologies were released in this period. To put it another way, we may refer to Web 2.5 as the confluence of the social and semantic webs.

Tell me about yourself.  This is the first question asked in most of the interviews. Do you know what to reply?  This is an opportunity to highlight your skills and showcase yourself.  Start with the most important thing that interviewer is expecting.  ✨How to answer this question? 1. Start with your name 2. Experience or Internship 3. If you are a fresher then mention your Qualification 4. Mention your Skillset/Tool Set (Highlight those skills which are mentioned in the Job description) 5. If the Interview does not stop you then you can mention your last project and your roles and responsibilities 6. Don’t mention skills in which you don’t have experience. If the interviewer starts asking questions about that skill, then you will be in trouble  ✨Ex. My Name is <Your Name>. I have <Yrs> of experience. (Or I have done an internship in <Company>). I have done my Engineering/BE/ME/MCA from <College name>. I am a Java Full Stack Developer. (Or I am looking for a Java Full Stack Developer role). I have worked on Java 8, Spring, Hibernate, Web Services, Bootstrap, and Angular JS.  Similar way, you can prepare your answer as per your career aspiration or role you are looking for.  ✨Practice makes you better. So, practice answering this question. It will develop your confidence. Do follow Nikhil Chaudhari for more such content 💯  You can join my free channels to get more job-related posts. Here we post Java-related Job Opportunities and articles that will help you to become an Interview ready.      Links are given in the comments. 👇  All the best! #interviewtips #interviewpreparation #interviewadvice #fresher #jobsearch #jobsearch

Which of the following resume statements do you think will resonate the best with employers? A or B?A: Managed a team and delivered new marketing initiatives orB: Directed a national team of 10 to deliver a new marketing initiative one month ahead of scheduleA: Responsible for all aspects of project management, including scheduling, budgeting, and logisticsorB: Delivered 6 oil and gas projects on time and within budget in 2021 by creating a standardized roadmap and processesA: Fostered communications across departments to increase employee engagementorB: Escalated employee engagement 45% in 6 months after initiating weekly team meetings and creating new KPI targetsA: Improved operational processes to save money orB: Delivered $1.4M in annual cost savings after optimizing operational processes and procedures across 4 facilities -------------I hope the answer is obvious. The A statements tell you something that almost anyone could claim.The B statements sell with specifics and quantitative results that back up the claim and provide more value to the reader.Sell, don't tell, by ensuring your resume includes more B statements.Looking for more examples of strong resume statements? Check out this resource I helped create: https://lnkd.in/gZEDqz9V#resume #executiveresume #executivesearch #jobsearch

🤷‍♀️When you apply for your dream job and don’t get an offer, the first thing you want to know is WHY.But that’s not always easy to tell - especially if, ultimately, you were ghosted 👻😡Often times we internalize the outcome as proof that we don’t measure up - which can be confidence crushing.But Judy Schoenberg 🦋 and I know there are so many other, more likely reasons why this opportunity didn’t pan out for you. ✔️the company may have gone with an internal hire✔️the company was ALWAYS going with an internal hire✔️you aren’t a culture fit. If this was the reason, count yourself lucky that the interviewer picked up on that. And save yourself a lot of pain later on!✔️you were qualified for the role, but you didn’t connect your qualifications to the job. It’s so important to connect the dots for employers. This is something you can improve upon next time!✔️the scope of the role changed after it was posted✔️the posting was canceledRejection is no fun. But it can be something to learn from rather than a confidence killer. Check out this  Harvard Business Review article’s tips below to grow from the experience:💫 realize there is no perfect job💫 step back and reflect on your career vision and values💫use this time to further sharpen your interviewing skills - are you connecting your accomplishments to the role?💫 ask for feedback from the recruiter 💫 become stronger and more resilient. There are many great roles out there!  Staying positive and growing from all experiences is crucial to launching your next, best chapter! To your success!#confidence #careerchange #jobsearch #careeradvice

What do you do with a MBA?Consulting, of course.It might get you into the boardroom and you might get to fly business class.But you also get into the detail and get your hands dirty.Very dirty.And if you want to build things that’s a must.Especially a business career as an engineer.I quickly worked out that consulting wasn’t just a job, it was a febrile training ground where I got paid to learn!Job No. 3️⃣ When I graduated from business school, consulting was the only thing I thought about.It was the 90s, everybody did.But not management consulting, IT consulting.See, the thing is, management doesn’t grow.In fact, in many organisations, it shrinks.But technology does…So I replied to another ad in another newspaper.Newspaper ads were fast becoming my friend. Well written cover letters (I was shown how) and interesting CVs (mine wasn’t especially impressive) were opening doors.Soon I was an IT consultant.Jeff Bezos left his job in New York to surf the big break we call the internet. 28 years later, Amazon is still around…I left business school about the same time to paddle out and catch my first wave.And, just like Amazon, 28 years later, I’m still around too.Because I learned how to build systems, at scale.I’ve never stopped.It’s one of my tools of trade. Lessons:1/ Go for growth. Track the the things that are growing and the things are going to explode and just like me and Jeff*, jump on board.2/ Become famous for something. Build your reputation around a killer competency and it becomes your professional passport. You can go anywhere, do anything and just bolt the business stuff on as you go.*That’s basically where the similarities end.#tech #job #jobsearch #jobsearchstrategies #career #engineering #engineer #engineers #chemicalengineering #careeradvice #security #chemicalengineer #emergingengineers #youngengineers #youngprofessionals #amazon #mba #consulting #managementconsulting #itconsulting #businessschool #graduateschool #monashuniversity

There is a theory that cold countries have more and better access to water bodies than hot countries. The access to water bodies allowed them to transport efficiently, and that’s what made them richer. Makes sense?⁠⁠Another theory is that it is easier for people to deal with a cold climate than a hot one. So if you are feeling cold, put on some clothes, but if you are feeling hot, you need to do more than remove clothes. This, in turn, could have led to a difference in work output. Makes sense?⁠⁠What do you think could be a valid explanation for this observation? Or is it just a coincidence? There are several methods to improve your CRS score while waiting in the Express Entry pool:Work on your weak areasMaintain a broad view and avoid being overly focused on one element at the expense of being aware of all the areas where points might be raised. Try to strengthen your weak areas while increasing your overall score. A slight improvement in two or three categories can significantly improve your chances for an ITA.Provincial nominationTry to gain 600 more points through a provincial nomination. These 600 points might be the difference between receiving an ITA or simply having to wait another six months. In addition, candidates who have already visited a province can earn bonus points, which is another thing to consider.Get a job offerObtaining a job offer will help you get 200 points while significantly enhancing your chances of receiving an ITA. The easiest method to do this is to undertake a thorough job search that is related to visiting Canada.Get help from an immigration expertConsider employing a professional in the immigration field. They can assist you in strengthening your digital resume, presenting you with an extensive database of possible hiring employers throughout Canada, and giving additional tips that will boost your immigration prospects. #hiring #work #job #jobsearch #help #database #immigration # #canada #resume #irelandjobs #canadaworkpermit #canadiancitizenship #expressentry #ukvisa #ieltspreparation #ieltsscore #oetpreparation

Singaporean wanted by US over North Korea is in Singapore: PoliceA Singaporean businessman wanted by the US for violating sanctions on North Korea is currently in the city-state where he is under investigation, the Singapore police said.For the latest headlines, follow our Google News channel online or via the app.In a statement issued late Saturday, the Singapore Police Force (SPF) said they have sought clarification from their US counterparts over the reward as they have kept them informed about the ongoing probe by local authorities.The US State Department on Thursday offered $5 million for information on businessman Kwek Kee Seng, blaming him for numerous fuel deliveries to North Korea and ship-to-ship transfers as well as money laundering through front companies.Federal prosecutors in New York in 2021 issued an arrest warrant for Kwek, a year after one of his oil tankers, the M/T Courageous, was seized by Cambodia on a US request over purported sanctions violations.Kwek, 62, owns the Swanseas Port Services shipping company based in the city-state.The State Department’s Rewards for Justice program had said his exact location was not known and that he has also been identified as being in North Korea, Cambodia, Taiwan and Thailand as well as Cameroon and the tiny Caribbean nation of Saint Kitts and Nevis.But Singapore’s police said in their statement that “Kwek is presently in Singapore.”He has been under investigation since April last year by the Commercial Affairs Department -- the city’s white-collar crime investigation agency -- and his passport has been impounded.The Singapore police said the investigation was launched after the US Justice Department announced a criminal complaint had been filed against Kwek for “allegedly conspiring to evade economic sanctions” on North Korea and for money laundering.Police added that they have shared information about their investigation of Kwek with US law enforcement authorities.“Since then, there were several more exchanges. Due to the nature and complexity of the case, investigations are still ongoing,” police said.“On 4 November 2022, the SPF wrote to our US counterparts to seek clarification, given that we had been in active communication with our US counterparts on Kwek’s case,” it added.“Singapore will continue to assist the US authorities within the ambit of our laws and international obligations.”The reward comes as the US urges strict enforcement of United Nations sanctions on North Korea after it launched a volley of missiles, including one that landed close to South Korea’s waters.Read more:US offers reward for Singaporean businessman over North Korea oil shipmentsShell signs MoU to explore carbon transport, storage options in Brunei and SingaporeSingapore proposes borrowing ban to fund crypto purchaseshttps://ift.tt/Gy7riJXhttps://ift.tt/aOKidfC#careers #hiring #job #interview #recruitment #hiring #jobs #jobsearch #recruiting #careers #hr ...

Dozens injured after fire in New York City: ReportAt least 38 people were injured in a fire in a New York City apartment building that may have been caused by a lithium ion battery, officials told US media on Saturday.For the latest headlines, follow our Google News channel online or via the app.Two of the wounded were in critical condition and five were seriously injured after the blaze on East 52nd Street in Manhattan, CNN quoted fire commissioner Laura Kavanagh as saying.Dan Flynn, chief fire marshal, told CNN it was nearly the 200th fire this year caused by a lithium-ion battery from a micromobility device. Such small, light electric vehicles can include e-bikes and electric scooters.“We’ve had six fatalities this year just from these batteries that power micromobility devices,” CNN quoted him as saying.Flynn said authorities believe the occupant of the apartment where the fire likely began had been repairing bikes in the building.Read more:Tanzania deploys army to battle Mount Kilimanjaro Nurses vote to strike in UK first: ReportNurses across the UK have voted to strike in their first national action over a pay dispute, a media report said on Sunday.For the latest headlines, follow our Google News channel online or via the app.The strike ballot among more than 300,000 members of the Royal College of Nursing (RCN) was the biggest in the union’s 106-year history.“Our strike action will be as much for patients as it is for nurses -- we have their support in doing this,” secretary Pat Cullen said.Although counting is still underway, the domestic PA news agency reported that RCN officials believed enough members had voted for winter industrial action, which is set to take place within a few weeks, possibly before Christmas.The RCN is campaigning for a pay rise of five percent above the soaring inflation.The exact nature of the strike is yet to be determined, but is likely to disrupt operations and appointments even as patients are already facing record waiting lists.“This will see the majority of services taken out, and picket lines across the country,” a union source told the Observer newspaper.It also comes as Prime Minister Rishi Sunak and Chancellor Jeremy Hunt already face the huge challenge of tackling a 50 billion pound ($57 billion) hole in public finances.The UK, which is struggling with a cost of living crisis, has seen a wave of industrial action in recent months.Tens of thousands of staff in various industries -- from the postal and legal systems to ports and telecommunications -- have gone one strike across Britain since the summer.The RCN said there were record nursing vacancies as 25,000 nursing staff around the UK left the Nursing and Midwifery Council register in the last year.Recent analysis showed an experienced nurse’s salary has fallen by 20 percent in real terms since 2010, and the RCN said the goodwill and expertise of nursing staff was being “exploited” by governments across the UK.Read more:Millions of UK nationals skipping meals in cost of living crisis: PollAmnesty seeks inquiry into COVID-19 deaths in Italian nursing homesUK’s largest nursing union begin biggest strike ballot in more than 100 New Zealand’s PM Ardern unveils childcare subsidy in cost-of-living packageNew Zealand Prime Minister Jacinda Ardern announced a cost-of-living package for families battling surging inflation, and she warned that 2023 will be more difficult “in many ways than this year.”More than half of New Zealand’s families with children will become eligible for subsidized childcare assistance from April 1, including all sole parents, Ardern said. The government will spend NZ$189 million ($112 million) to increase the income threshold for assistance in the program, reversing a freeze imposed in 2010.For the latest headlines, follow our Google News channel online or via the app.More than 10,000 additional children will be eligible for support, the prime minister said at a Labor leader’s party conference speech in Auckland Sunday.The announcement comes as Ardern’s Labor Party faces the prospect of a by-election in coming months after rebel member of parliament Gaurav Sharma announced he is resigning. A by-election will be a test of Labor's support ahead of the next general election, expected to be held in late 2023.“Front and center right now, we have the extraordinary challenges of a cost-of-living crisis, global in origin but affecting many Kiwis,” Ardern said. “Right now, the load for families across New Zealand is a heavy one, and while there are many pressures, we know childcare is the biggest in-work expense for families.”The policy means a family with two parents both working 40 hours per week on NZ$26 per hour with two children under five will now become eligible for NZ$252 per week from April 2023.Ardern said New Zealand women cannot afford to work if they want to because of childcare costs and they are forgoing NZ$116 million or more in wages every year.“This barrier to work exacerbates a workforce shortage, but more than that, it removes the ability for many New Zealand families to choose what’s best for them,” she added.Read more:New Zealand suspends bilateral human rights dialog with IranNew Zealand PM visits Antarctica to highlight climate change challengesNew Zealand influencers relieved after being released from detention in Iranhttps://ift.tt/J9adl5g#careers #hiring #job #interview #recruitment #hiring #jobs #jobsearch #recruiting #careers #hr #employment #resume #humanresources #qatar #uae #employment #jobs #jobsearch #hiring #job #recruitment #career #work #careers #Automobile #Accounting #Automobilejobs #recruiting #nowhiring #jobopening #recruiter #jobinterview #vacancy #Qatar #dubai #KSA #Oman #hr #AnyGulfJobs AnyGulfJobs.com #abudhabi #oil #jobvacancies #gas #OilandGas #OilandGasjobs #ConstructionJobs #wearehiring #employment #jobs #applyonline #recruiting #job #opportunity #wearerecruiting #qatarjobs #nowhiring #hiring #recruitment #employmentopportunities #careers #hr #help #comment #like #network #unitedarabemirates #vacancies #share #education #computerscience #science #chemistry #school #teacher...

Britain to hold public holiday for King Charles’ coronationA public holiday will be held to mark the coronation of King Charles III in May, eight months after the death of his mother Queen Elizabeth II, the British government said Sunday.For the latest headlines, follow our Google News channel online or via the app.The national holiday will be held on Monday May 8, two days after the ceremony at Westminster Abbey, Downing Street said in a statement.The government said that as with the coronation of Queen Elizabeth II in 1953, the royal event would be an opportunity for “families and communities across the country to come together and celebrate.”King Charles, 73, will be formally crowned at London’s Westminster Abbey, following a long tradition dating back more than 900 years.The monarch’s wife, Queen Consort Camilla, 75, will also be crowned.Prime Minister Rishi Sunak said it would be “a unique moment for our country.”“In recognition of this historic occasion, I am pleased to announce an additional bank holiday for the whole United Kingdom next year,” he said, according to the statement.The coronation traditionally takes place some months after a new sovereign has ascended to the throne, following a period of national and royal mourning as well as intense preparation.Buckingham Palace has said the coronation will reflect the monarchy’s historic traditions and its modern role.Charles immediately became king when Queen Elizabeth died on September 8. He also took over as head of state of 14 Commonwealth countries, including Australia, Canada and New Zealand.The Queen, who was 96, died at her remote Scottish estate Balmoral after a year of declining health. What do you do with a MBA?Consulting, of course.It might get you into the boardroom and you might get to fly business class.But you also get into the detail and get your hands dirty.Very dirty.And if you want to build things that’s a must.Especially a business career as an engineer.I quickly worked out that consulting wasn’t just a job, it was a febrile training ground where I got paid to learn!Job No. 3️⃣ When I graduated from business school, consulting was the only thing I thought about.It was the 90s, everybody did.But not management consulting, IT consulting.See, the thing is, management doesn’t grow.In fact, in many organisations, it shrinks.But technology does…So I replied to another ad in another newspaper.Newspaper ads were fast becoming my friend. Well written cover letters (I was shown how) and interesting CVs (mine wasn’t especially impressive) were opening doors.Soon I was an IT consultant.Jeff Bezos left his job in New York to surf the big break we call the internet. 28 years later, Amazon is still around…I left business school about the same time to paddle out and catch my first wave.And, just like Amazon, 28 years later, I’m still around too.Because I learned how to build systems, at scale.I’ve never stopped.It’s one of my tools of trade. Lessons:1/ Go for growth. Track the the things that are growing and the things are going to explode and just like me and Jeff*, jump on board.2/ Become famous for something. Build your reputation around a killer competency and it becomes your professional passport. You can go anywhere, do anything and just bolt the business stuff on as you go.*That’s basically where the similarities end.#tech #job #jobsearch #jobsearchstrategies #career #engineering #engineer #engineers #chemicalengineering #careeradvice #security #chemicalengineer #emergingengineers #youngengineers #youngprofessionals #amazon #mba #consulting #managementconsulting #itconsulting #businessschool #graduateschool #monashuniversity
